# Text Elements
When the bonds in water become rigid, they take up more space 
than the free flowing and easily breakable bonds it is made up 
of in its liquid state ^TcGzv0xh

Clearly solids are more
dense than liquids ^BxXxgyUZ

```json
			"name": true,
			"outline": true
		}
	},
	"files": {}
}
```
